    "/*
    This file was generated from ion source. Do not edit.
    */
    import * as Expression from './Expression';
    import * as Statement from './Statement';
    import * as Node from './Node';
    import * as Null from '../ion/Null';
    import * as String from '../ion/String';
    import * as Class from '../ion/Class';
    export class Declaration {
        readonly name: Node.ShortName;
        readonly type: Expression.Expression | Null.Null;
        readonly name: Node.ShortName;
        readonly id: String.String;
        constructor({name, type = null, name, id}: {
            name: Node.ShortName,
            type?: Expression.Expression | Null.Null,
            name: Node.ShortName,
            id: String.String
        }) {
            if (!Node.isShortName(name))
                throw new Error('name is not a ShortName: ' + name);
            if (!(Expression.isExpression(type) || Null.isNull(type)))
                throw new Error('type is not a Expression | Null: ' + type);
            if (!Node.isShortName(name))
                throw new Error('name is not a ShortName: ' + name);
            if (!String.isString(id))
                throw new Error('id is not a String: ' + id);
            this.name = name;
            this.type = type;
            this.name = name;
            this.id = id;
        }
        static is(value): value is Declaration {
            return isDeclaration(value);
        }
    }
    Declaration['id'] = 'sample_Declaration';
    Declaration['implements'] = new Set([
        'sample_Declaration',
        'sample_Expression',
        'sample_Statement',
        'sample_Node',
        'sample_Node'
    ]);
    export const isDeclaration = function (value): value is Declaration {
        return Class.isInstance(Declaration, value);
    };"

            if (!(isExpression(type) || Null.isNull(type)))
                throw new Error('type is not a Expression | Null: ' + type);
            this.name = name;
            this.type = type;

        static is(value): value is Expression {

  • sample/Node.ts
    "/*
    This file was generated from ion source. Do not edit.
    */
    import * as String from '../ion/String';
    import * as Class from '../ion/Class';
    type ShortName = String.String;
    function isShortName(value): value is ShortName {
        return String.isString(value) && (value.length > 0 && value.length < 100);
    }
    export class Node {
        readonly name: ShortName;
        constructor({name}: { name: ShortName }) {
            if (!isShortName(name))
                throw new Error('name is not a ShortName: ' + name);
            this.name = name;
        }
        static is(value): value is Node {
            return isNode(value);
        }
    }
    Node['id'] = 'sample_Node';
    Node['implements'] = new Set(['sample_Node']);
    export const isNode = function (value): value is Node {
        return Class.isInstance(Node, value);
    };"
